^quang|r ^ninh| se|x di| doi|wf cac|s co|w so|wr tieu|zr thu|r cong|z nghiep|zj ra| khoi|r khu| dan|z cu|w
^quang|r ^ninh| dda|x co|w ban|r hoan|f thien|zj ^dde|zf an|s ddon|w vi|j hanh|f chinh|s kinh| te|zs ddac|wj biet|zj ^van|z ^ddon|zf

^dday|f ddoa|j nhau| vi|f ddiem|zr so|zs

# ^ngay|f hoi|zj tong|f quan|z #
